\section*{Puzzle 5}

\vspace{0.5cm}
\begin{center}
\begin{tikzpicture}[x={0.7\textwidth/8},y={0.7\textwidth/8}]
\fill (0,7) rectangle (1,8);
\fill (1,7) rectangle (2,8);

\draw (5,7) rectangle (6,8);

\end{enumerate}
